1.2 Tạo Labeling Guidelines ^Rgz3qpzF

Tommy tạo một Guideline document

Guideline Record:
{
  guidelineId: "GUIDE_001",
  projectId: "PROJ_001",
  title: "Pneumonia Classification Guidelines v1.0",
  content: "
    - Normal: Clear lung fields, no infiltrates
    - Bacterial Pneumonia: Dense consolidation, lobar pattern
    - Viral Pneumonia: Bilateral interstitial infiltrates
    - COVID-19: Ground-glass opacities, peripheral distribution
    - Uncertain: Request senior review
  ",
  version: 1,
  createdAt: "2024-01-15 09:15:00"
} ^EeKqN6t1
